Retail Demand Forecasting & Inventory Optimization¶

Phase-1 :- Data Understanding¶

Objective¶

To understand the structure, quality, and characteristics of the M5 Forecasting Dataset before performing data cleaning, exploratory data analysis, feature engineering, and demand forecasting.

In [1]:
# Import Required libraries
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

pd.set_option("display.max_columns", None)
pd.set_option("display.max_rows", 100)
In [2]:
# Load Datasets
calendar = pd.read_csv(r"C:\Users\LENOVO\Desktop\Zalima Development Project 2\Retail Demand Forecasting & Inventory optimization\data\raw\calendar.csv")

sales = pd.read_csv(r"C:\Users\LENOVO\Desktop\Zalima Development Project 2\Retail Demand Forecasting & Inventory optimization\data\raw\sales_train_validation.csv")

prices = pd.read_csv(r"C:\Users\LENOVO\Desktop\Zalima Development Project 2\Retail Demand Forecasting & Inventory optimization\data\raw\sell_prices.csv")

submission = pd.read_csv(r"C:\Users\LENOVO\Desktop\Zalima Development Project 2\Retail Demand Forecasting & Inventory optimization\data\raw\sample_submission.csv")

evaluation = pd.read_csv(r"C:\Users\LENOVO\Desktop\Zalima Development Project 2\Retail Demand Forecasting & Inventory optimization\data\raw\sales_train_evaluation.csv")

The M5 dataset consists of five files: calendar, sales, sell prices, sample submission, and evaluation data. The sales dataset contains 30,490 products with daily sales records across 1,913 days. The data follows a hierarchical structure from state → store → category → department → item, making it suitable for retail demand forecasting and inventory optimization. The calendar dataset provides event and seasonal information, while the sell prices dataset enables price-based demand analysis.

sales = pd.read_csv(r"C:\Users\LENOVO\Desktop\Zalima Development Project 2\Retail Demand Forecasting & Inventory optimization\data\raw\sales_train_validation.csv")

prices = pd.read_csv(r"C:\Users\LENOVO\Desktop\Zalima Development Project 2\Retail Demand Forecasting & Inventory optimization\data\raw\sell_prices.csv")

Data Understanding Summary¶

Project Overview¶

The objective of this project is to forecast future product demand and support inventory optimization using Walmart's M5 Forecasting dataset. Historical sales, pricing information, calendar events, and seasonal patterns will be analyzed to build demand forecasting models and generate inventory-related insights.

Datasets Used¶

1. Calendar Dataset¶

  • Shape: (1969, 14)
  • Contains date-level information.
  • Includes weekdays, months, years, events, holidays, and SNAP program indicators.
  • Used for seasonality and event-based demand analysis.

2. Sales Train Validation Dataset¶

  • Shape: (30490, 1919)
  • Main forecasting dataset.
  • Contains daily sales history for each product-store combination.
  • Sales columns range from d_1 to d_1913.

3. Sell Prices Dataset¶

  • Shape: (6841121, 4)
  • Contains weekly product prices.
  • Used to analyze price impact on demand.

4. Sample Submission Dataset¶

  • Competition-specific file.
  • Not required for this portfolio project.

5. Sales Train Evaluation Dataset¶

  • Competition evaluation file.
  • Not required for current forecasting workflow.

Business Hierarchy¶

The dataset follows the following retail hierarchy:

State → Store → Category → Department → Product

Category Analysis¶

Total Categories: 3

  • FOODS
  • HOUSEHOLD
  • HOBBIES

Category Distribution:

Category Records
FOODS 14,370
HOUSEHOLD 10,470
HOBBIES 5,650

Department Analysis¶

Total Departments: 7

  • FOODS_1
  • FOODS_2
  • FOODS_3
  • HOBBIES_1
  • HOBBIES_2
  • HOUSEHOLD_1
  • HOUSEHOLD_2

State Analysis¶

Total States: 3

  • CA (California)
  • TX (Texas)
  • WI (Wisconsin)

State Distribution:

State Records
CA 12,196
TX 9,147
WI 9,147

Store Analysis¶

Total Stores: 10

  • CA_1
  • CA_2
  • CA_3
  • CA_4
  • TX_1
  • TX_2
  • TX_3
  • WI_1
  • WI_2
  • WI_3

Each store contains 3,049 product records.

Product Analysis¶

  • Total Unique Products: 3,049
  • Total Product-Store Combinations: 30,490

One row in the sales dataset represents:

Product + Store + Daily Sales History

Historical Coverage¶

Date Range:

  • Start Date: 2011-01-29
  • End Date: 2016-06-19

Approximate historical coverage:

  • More than 5 years of sales data

Missing Values Analysis¶

Calendar dataset contains missing values in:

  • event_name_1
  • event_type_1
  • event_name_2
  • event_type_2

These missing values are expected because events occur only on selected dates. They do not represent data quality issues.

Sales Data Observations¶

Descriptive statistics indicate:

  • No missing sales values.
  • Large number of zero-sales observations.
  • Highly sparse demand patterns.
  • Significant variation across products.
  • Presence of intermittent demand, which is common in retail forecasting datasets.

Forecasting Datasets Selected¶

The following datasets will be used in the forecasting pipeline:

  • sales_train_validation.csv
  • calendar.csv
  • sell_prices.csv

Competition-related files are excluded from further analysis.

Conclusion¶

The dataset provides a rich retail hierarchy with more than five years of historical sales data, pricing information, and event-based calendar features. The data structure is suitable for demand forecasting, trend analysis, seasonality detection, and inventory optimization. The next phase of the project will focus on data cleaning, preprocessing, and preparation for forecasting models.
